# ::id dip_test_0001.1
# ::snt ITALY said to AUSTRIA: Hey Austria! I know AT is one of the least successful alliances in the game, so I'm super down to work together here, especially if we can get Russia and Turkey fighting.
(a / and
      :op1 (a2 / ally-01
            :ARG1 (a3 / and
                  :op1 (c / country
                        :name (n / name
                              :op1 "Italy"))
                  :op2 (c2 / country
                        :name (n2 / name
                              :op1 "Austria"))))
      :op2 (p / propose-01
            :ARG0 c
            :ARG1 a2
            :ARG1 (a4 / and
                  :op1 c
                  :op2 c2)
            :ARG3 (a5 / and
                  :op1 (c3 / country
                        :name (n3 / name
                              :op1 "Russia"))
                  :op2 (c4 / country
                        :name (n4 / name
                              :op1 "Turkey"))))
      :ARG3 c2)

# ::id dip_test_0001.2
# ::snt FRANCE said to GERMANY: Hey Germany! Just reaching out to say I think our two nations tend to benefit a ton from working together, and I'm very down to work together if you'd be interested!
(a / and
      :op1 (t / tell-01
            :ARG0 (c / country
                  :name (n / name
                        :op1 "France"))
            :ARG1 (p / propose-01
                  :ARG0 (c2 / country
                        :name (n2 / name
                              :op1 "Germany"))
                  :ARG1 (a2 / ally-01
                        :ARG1 (a3 / and
                              :op1 c
                              :op2 (c3 / country
                                    :name (n3 / name
                                          :op1 "England"))))
                  :ARG3 c)
            :ARG2 c3)
      :op2 (p2 / propose-01
            :ARG0 c
            :ARG1 a2
            :ARG1 (a4 / and
                  :op1 c3
                  :op2 c2))
      :ARG3 c2)

# ::id dip_test_0001.3
# ::snt FRANCE said to ITALY: Hey Italy! I think our two nations tend to do best when we can leave each other alone, so I'd love it if we could agree to not harass one another?
(a / and
      :op1 (t / tell-01
            :ARG0 (c / country
                  :name (n / name
                        :op1 "France"))
            :ARG1 (p / propose-01
                  :ARG0 (c2 / country
                        :name (n2 / name
                              :op1 "Italy"))
                  :ARG1 (a2 / attack-01
                        :polarity -
                        :ARG0 (a3 / and
                              :op1 c
                              :op2 c2)
                        :ARG1 (c3 / country
                              :name (n3 / name
                                    :op1 "Germany")))
                  :ARG3 c)
            :ARG2 c3)
      :op2 (p2 / propose-01
            :ARG0 c2
            :ARG1 (a4 / attack-01
                  :ARG0 (a5 / and
                        :op1 c
                        :op2 c2)
                  :ARG1 c3)
            :ARG3 c))

# ::id dip_test_0001.4
# ::snt GERMANY said to FRANCE: Hey France, absolutely! Are you up for a DMZ in Burgundy?
(a / and
      :op1 (t / tell-01
            :ARG0 (c / country
                  :name (n / name
                        :op1 "Germany"))
            :ARG1 (d / demilitarize-01
                  :ARG1 a
                  :op1 c
                  :op2 (c2 / country
                        :name (n2 / name
                              :op1 "France")))
            :ARG2 (s / sea
                  :name (n3 / name
                        :op1 "English"
                        :op2 "Channel")))
      :ARG2 c2
      :op2 (p / propose-01
            :ARG0 c
            :ARG1 d
            :ARG1 a
            :op1 c2
            :op2 c)
      :ARG2 (p2 / province
            :name (n4 / name
                  :op1 "Burgundy"))
      :ARG3 c2)

# ::id dip_test_0001.5
# ::snt TURKEY said to RUSSIA: Hey Russia, just wanna say good luck and hopefully we can be friends!
(t / tell-01
      :ARG0 (c / country
            :name (n / name
                  :op1 "Austria"))
      :ARG1 (p / propose-01

                  :name (n2 / name
                        :op1 "Russia"))

                  :ARG1 (a2 / and
                        :op1 c
                        :op2 c2))
            :ARG3 (c3 / country
                  :name (n3 / name
                        :op1 "Italy")))
      :ARG2 c3)

# ::id dip_test_0001.6
# ::snt AUSTRIA said to ITALY: I'm also down! Have you heard from either of them yet?
(a / agree-01
      :ARG0 (c / country
            :name (n / name
                  :op1 "Austria"))
      :ARG2 (c2 / country
            :name (n2 / name
                  :op1 "Italy")))

# ::id dip_test_0001.7
# ::snt ENGLAND said to FRANCE: Hey France! I think we both have bigger concerns than each other so I'd like to propose an alliance between us. Would you be willing to agree to a DMZ in the Channel?
(a / and
      :op1 (t / tell-01
            :ARG0 (c / country
                  :name (n / name
                        :op1 "England"))
            :ARG1 (p / propose-01
                  :ARG0 (c2 / country
                        :name (n2 / name
                              :op1 "Germany"))
                  :ARG1 (a2 / ally-01
                        :ARG1 (a3 / and
                              :op1 c
                              :op2 c2))
                  :ARG3 (c3 / country
                        :name (n3 / name
                              :op1 "France")))
            :op2 (p2 / propose-01
                  :ARG0 c
                  :ARG1 (d / demilitarize-01
                        :ARG1 (a4 / and
                              :op1 c
                              :op2 c2)
                        :ARG2 (s / sea
                              :name (n4 / name
                                    :op1 "English"
                                    :op2 "Channel")))
                  :ARG3 c2)))

# ::id dip_test_0001.8
# ::snt AUSTRIA said to RUSSIA: Hi Russia, good luck this game! Would you be interested in working together? Do you want to bounce Galicia?
(a / and
      :op1 (p / propose-01
            :ARG0 (c / country
                  :name (n / name
                        :op1 "Austria"))
            :ARG1 (a2 / ally-01
                  :ARG1 (a3 / and
                        :op1 c

                              :name (n2 / name
                                    :op1 "Russia"))))
            :ARG3 (c3 / country
                  :name (n3 / name
                        :op1 "Italy")))
      :op2 (p2 / propose-01
            :ARG0 c
            :ARG1 (b / bounce-03
                  :ARG1 (u / unit
                        :mod c)
                  :ARG2 (u2 / unit
                        :mod c2)
                  :ARG3 (p3 / province
                        :name (n4 / name
                              :op1 "Galicia")))
            :ARG3 c2))

# ::id dip_test_0001.18
# ::snt ITALY said to RUSSIA: Hey Russia! I love an R/I, and I think it's one of the more effective alliances in the game. What do you say we work together to take out Turkey and then Austria?

      :op1 (p / propose-01
            :ARG0 (c / country
                  :name (n / name

                              :name (n2 / name

                        :op3 (c3 / country
                              :name (n3 / name
                                    :op1 "Austria")))
                  :ARG3 (c4 / country
                        :name (n4 / name
                              :op1 "Turkey")))

      :op2 (p2 / propose-01
            :ARG0 c2
            :ARG1 (a4 / ally-01

                        :op1 c2
                        :op2 c4)
                  :ARG3 (a6 / and
                        :op1 (c5 / country
                              :name (n5 / name
                                    :op1 "Turkey"))
                        :op2 (c6 / country
                              :name (n6 / name
                                    :op1 "Italy"))))
            :ARG3 c4))

# ::id dip_test_0001.19
# ::snt ENGLAND said to RUSSIA: Hey Russia! I'd like to take Norway this year, but I'm not planning on sending any further units your way. If there's anything I can do to help you, feel free to ask!

      :op1 (p / propose-01
            :ARG0 (c / country
                  :name (n / name
                        :op1 "England"))

                  :ARG0 c
                  :ARG1 (p2 / province
                        :name (n2 / name
                              :op1 "Norway"))

                        :year 1906))
            :ARG3 (c2 / country
                  :name (n3 / name
                        :op1 "Russia")))
      :op2 (t / tell-01
            :polarity -
            :ARG0 c2
            :ARG1 (p3 / propose-01
                  :ARG0 c
                  :ARG1 h
                  :ARG0 c2
                  :ARG1 p2
                  :time d
                  :year 1906))
      :ARG2 c2)

                  :name (n4 / name
                        :op1 "Germany"))

# ::id dip_test_0001.31
# ::snt ENGLAND said to RUSSIA: I don't think I can do that; it would leave me completely open to France. However, I am planning on taking it with a fleet.
(a / and
      :op1 (r / reject-01
            :ARG0 (c / country
                  :name (n / name
                        :op1 "England"))
            :ARG1 (h / have-03
                  :ARG0 c
                  :ARG1 (p / province
                        :name (n2 / name
                              :op1 "Belgium"))))
      :op2 (t / tell-01
            :ARG0 (c2 / country
                  :name (n3 / name
                        :op1 "Russia"))
            :ARG1 (p2 / possible-01
                  :ARG1 (h2 / have-03
                        :ARG0 c
                        :ARG1 p
                        :instrument (f / fleet)))
            :ARG2 c))

# ::id dip_test_0001.32
# ::snt RUSSIA said to AUSTRIA: Hey Austria, sounds good to me! Bounce Galicia and work together sounds good to me, I think the R/A is one of the more powerful alliances on the board.

      :op1 (p / propose-01
            :ARG0 (c / country
                  :name (n / name
                        :op1 "Russia"))
            :ARG1 (b / bounce-03
                  :ARG1 (a2 / and
                        :op1 (u / unit
                              :mod c)
                        :op2 (u2 / unit
                              :mod (c2 / country
                                    :name (n2 / name
                                          :op1 "Austria"))))
                  :ARG3 (p2 / province
                        :name (n3 / name
                              :op1 "Galicia")))
            :ARG3 c2)
      :op2 (a3 / ally-01
            :ARG1 (a4 / and
                  :op1 c
                  :op2 c2)
            :ARG3 (a5 / and
                  :op1 (c3 / country
                        :name (n4 / name
                              :op1 "Italy"))
                  :op2 c2)))

# ::id dip_test_0001.38
# ::snt ENGLAND said to FRANCE: Let's do an E/F against Germany. I'd like a second build this year, though. Do you mind supporting me into Belgium?
(a / and
      :op1 (p / propose-01
            :ARG0 (c / country
                  :name (n / name
                        :op1 "England"))
            :ARG1 (a2 / and
                  :op1 (a3 / attack-01
                        :ARG0 (a4 / and
                              :op1 (c2 / country
                                    :name (n2 / name
                                          :op1 "France"))
                              :op2 (c3 / country
                                    :name (n3 / name
                                          :op1 "Italy")))
                        :ARG1 (c4 / country
                              :name (n4 / name
                                    :op1 "Germany")))
                  :op2 (b / build-01
                        :ARG0 c2
                        :ARG1 (u / unit)
                        :time (d / date-entity
                              :year 1904))
                  :ARG3 c2)
            :op2 (p2 / propose-01
                  :ARG0 c2
                  :ARG1 (s / support-01
                        :ARG0 c2
                        :ARG1 (m / move-01
                              :ARG1 u
                              :mod c2)
